A common solution is a personal CCTV device like this one - https://www.enhancedvision.com/shop/low-vision-products/acrobat-hd-ultra-lcd That seemed to me like ancient technology. These devices use insanely expensive optical zoom cameras (x4-x80) with up to 720p resolution. The FOV is limited as well so the user must continuously change the camera orientation by hand. Try to do that while following a teacher writing on a backboard, zooming in and out to read and navigate and actually pay attention to what's going on in class...\r\n\r\nI had another idea.
